18/03/24, 3:40â€¯pm - Chandani Vanani LD: Mechanical 603
18/03/24, 6:10â€¯pm - Diya Patel LD: Event Description:
"Market Madness" is an offline stock market simulation where participants have the opportunity to buy and sell stocks of various sub-events happening simultaneously in the larger finance literary event. Participants act as investors, aiming to make profitable investment decisions based on the performance of the sub-events.

How it Works:

Sub-Events as Stock Options:

Each sub-event within the finance literary event is treated as a stock option.
Sub-events can include competitions, workshops, seminars, or any activity happening during the event.
Initial Stock Offering (ISO):

Prior to the event, organizers assign an initial value to each sub-event stock based on factors like popularity, anticipated attendance, and relevance.
Participants are provided with virtual currency (e.g., play money) to invest in these stocks.
Trading Session:

During designated trading sessions within the event, participants can buy, sell, or hold stocks of the sub-events.
Real-time updates on the progress and outcomes of sub-events are provided to participants.
Profit/Loss Calculation:

At the end of the event, the performance of each sub-event is evaluated.
Participants' profits or losses are calculated based on the change in value of the stocks they hold.
The participant with the highest portfolio value or profit is declared the winner.
Requirements:

Stock Market Board: A large display or bulletin board where the values of sub-event stocks are updated in real-time.
Play Money: Organizers provide participants with play money to invest in stocks.
Market Hours: Designated time slots during the event for trading sessions.
Event Monitoring: Volunteers or staff members to monitor the progress of sub-events and update stock values accordingly.
Prizes: Prizes or recognition for participants with the highest portfolio value or profit.
Benefits:

Engagement: Encourages active participation and engagement with various sub-events within the finance literary event.
Educational: Provides a practical understanding of stock market dynamics and investment strategies.
Competition: Adds a competitive element to the event, fostering excitement and camaraderie among participants.
Networking: Facilitates interaction and networking among participants as they discuss investment strategies and market trends.
"Market Madness" offers a dynamic and interactive way for participants to experience the excitement and challenges of stock market investment within the context of a larger finance literary event.
